        <div>
            <h1><i class="icon-soccer"></i>
                Fútbol                    <button class="js-favorite-button uk-button uk-button-mini uk-icon-star-o" data-type="sport" data-id="13" data-label="Fútbol" type="button" data-uk-tooltip="{pos:'right'}" title="Agregar o eliminar de favoritos"></button>
